itemprop="text"><h1 tabindex="-1" id="user-content-llm_arc_solver" dir="auto"><a class="heading-link" href="#llm_arc_solver">LLM_ARC_Solver<svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></h1>
<p dir="auto">This is an attempt to fine-tune an llm to solve François Chollet's Abstract Reasoning Corpus (ARC) Challenge.</p>
<p dir="auto">I am no expert in llm's.. just trying to see if this may be a plausible solution.</p>
<p dir="auto">Thank you to the following people whose blog posts helped get me started:</p>

<li><a href="https://adithyask.medium.com/a-beginners-guide-to-fine-tuning-mistral-7b-instruct-model-0f39647b20fe" rel="nofollow">https://adithyask.medium.com/a-beginners-guide-to-fine-tuning-mistral-7b-instruct-model-0f39647b20fe</a></li>
